///// FILE: "React/src/modules/authenticationSimulationDB.test.js"

import { describe, expect, it } from "@jest/globals";
import { authenticationSimulationDB } from "./authenticationSimulationDB";

describe("The authenticationSimulationDB function", () => {
  it("authenticates when email and password are correct", async () => {
    //ARRANGE
    const email = "aaa@aaa.com";
    const password = "aaa";

    //ACT
    const isAuthenticated = await authenticationSimulationDB(email, password);

    //ASSERT
    expect(isAuthenticated).toBe(true);
  });
  it("doesn't authenticate when the email is correct, but the password is wrong", async () => {
    //ARRANGE
    const email = "aaa@aaa.com";
    const password = "aaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa";

    //ACT
    const isAuthenticated = await authenticationSimulationDB(email, password);

    //ASSERT
    expect(isAuthenticated).toBe(false);
  });
  it("doesn't authenticate when the email is not in the list", async () => {
    //ARRANGE
    const email = "zzz@zzz.zzz";
    const password = "aaa";

    //ACT
    const isAuthenticated = await authenticationSimulationDB(email, password);

    //ASSERT
    expect(isAuthenticated).toBe(false);
  });
  it("doesn't authenticate when the email is in the list, but the password is empty", async () => {
    //ARRANGE
    const email = "aaa@aaa.com";
    const password = "";

    //ACT
    const isAuthenticated = await authenticationSimulationDB(email, password);

    //ASSERT
    expect(isAuthenticated).toBe(false);
  });
  it("doesn't authenticate when the email is empty, but the password is in the list", async () => {
    //ARRANGE
    const email = "";
    const password = "aaa";

    //ACT
    const isAuthenticated = await authenticationSimulationDB(email, password);

    //ASSERT
    expect(isAuthenticated).toBe(false);
  });
});


///// FILE: "React/src/modules/DatabaseSimulation.js"

export class DatabaseSimulation {
  secretKey = "xyz321";
  isConnected = false;

  constructor(apiKey = "") {
    // console.log(this.secretKey);
    // console.log(this.isConnected);

    const doesMatch = apiKey === this.secretKey;
    if (doesMatch) this.isConnected = true;
  }

  async getData(logins = [], email = "") {
    const matchingLogin = {};
    if (this.isConnected) {
      console.log(`I promise to find ${email} in ${logins}...`);
      console.log("getting data...");
      for (const login of logins) {
        const doesMatch = email === login.email;
        if (doesMatch) {
          matchingLogin.email = login.email;
          matchingLogin.password = login.password;
        }
      }
    } else {
      console.log("Database is not connected.");
    }

    return matchingLogin;
  }

  // getData(logins = [], email = "") {
  //   const promise = new Promise(findLogin);
  //   return promise;

  //   function findLogin(resolve) {
  //     const matchingLogin = {};

  //     THERE IS AN ERROR
  //     this IS NOT THE DATABASE OBJECT
  //     this IS THE FUNCTION OBJECT OF findLogin
  //     USE ASYNC AND AWAIT TO AVOID THIS MIXUP
  //     if (this.isConnected) {
  //       console.log(`I promise to find ${email} in ${logins}...`);
  //       console.log("getting data...");
  //       for (const login of logins) {
  //         const doesMatch = email === login.email;
  //         if (doesMatch) {
  //           matchingLogin.email = login.email;
  //           matchingLogin.password = login.password;
  //         }
  //       }
  //     } else {
  //       console.log("Database is not connected.");
  //     }
  //     resolve(matchingLogin);
  //   }
  // }
}

function correctApiKey() {
  //ARRANGE
  const apiKey = "xyz321";

  //ACT
  const client = new DatabaseSimulation(apiKey);

  //ASSERT
  expect(client.isConnected).toBe(true);
}

function wrongApiKey() {
  //ARRANGE
  const apiKey = "zzz789";

  //ACT
  const client = new DatabaseSimulation(apiKey);

  //ASSERT
  expect(client.isConnected).toBe(false);
}

function emptyApiKey() {
  //ARRANGE
  const apiKey = "";

  //ACT
  const client = new DatabaseSimulation(apiKey);

  //ASSERT
  expect(client.isConnected).toBe(false);
}

async function correctEmail() {
  //ARRANGE
  const apiKey = "xyz321";
  const client = new DatabaseSimulation(apiKey);
  const email = "aaa@aaa.com";

  //ACT

  //ASSERT

}

///// FILE: "React/src/utils/addition.js"

export function addition(x, y) {
  const result = Number(x) + Number(y);
  return result;
}


///// FILE: "React/src/utils/addition.test.js"

import { describe, expect, it, test } from "@jest/globals";
import { addition } from "./addition";

describe("The addition function...", () => {
  it("adds positive numbers", addPositives);
  it("adds a positive and negative number", addPositiveNegative);
  it("adds negative numbers", addNegatives);
  it("return NaN when strings are used", addStrings);
  it("adds number strings", addNumberStrings);
});

function addPositives() {
  //ARRANGE: Set the variables for the test
  const x = 3;
  const y = 4;

  //ACT: Use the unit with the variables
  const result = addition(x, y);

  //ASSERT: Check if the unit works as expected
  expect(result).toBe(7);
}

function addPositiveNegative() {
  //ARRANGE
  const x = 3;
  const y = -4;

  //ACT
  const result = addition(x, y);

  //ASSERT
  expect(result).toBe(-1);
}

function addNegatives() {
  //ARRANGE
  const x = -3;
  const y = -4;

  //ACT
  const result = addition(x, y);

  //ASSERT
  expect(result).toBe(-7);
}

function addStrings() {
  //ARRANGE
  const x = "dog";
  const y = "cat";

  //ACT
  const result = addition(x, y);

  //ASSERT
  expect(result).toBeNaN();
  // expect(result).toBe(NaN);
}

function addNumberStrings() {
  //ARRANGE
  const x = "3";
  const y = "4";

  //ACT
  const result = addition(x, y);

  //ASSERT
  expect(result).toBe(7);
}


///// FILE: "React/src/utils/output.js"

export function output(
  message = "",
  outputTag = "outputTag",
  shouldAppend = true
) {
  const element = document.getElementById(outputTag);
  if (shouldAppend) element.innerHTML += message;
  else element.innerHTML = message;
}

      <div className="carousel-indicators">
        <button
          type="button"
          data-bs-target="#myPictures"
          data-bs-slide-to="0"
          className="active"
          aria-current="true"
          aria-label="Slide 1"
        ></button>
        <button
          type="button"
          data-bs-target="#myPictures"
          data-bs-slide-to="1"
          aria-label="Slide 2"
        ></button>
        <button
          type="button"
          data-bs-target="#myPictures"
          data-bs-slide-to="2"
          aria-label="Slide 3"
        ></button>
      </div>
      <div className="carousel-inner">
        <div className="carousel-item active">
          <img src={baby} className="d-block w-100" alt="baby picture" />
        </div>
        <div className="carousel-item">
          <img src={shapes} className="d-block w-100" alt="2D shapes" />
        </div>
        <div className="carousel-item">
          <img src={newYear} className="d-block w-100" alt="New Year 2025" />
        </div>
      </div>
      <button
        className="carousel-control-prev"
        type="button"
        data-bs-target="#myPictures"
        data-bs-slide="prev"
      >
        <span className="carousel-control-prev-icon" aria-hidden="true"></span>
        <span className="visually-hidden">Previous</span>
      </button>
      <button
        className="carousel-control-next"
        type="button"
        data-bs-target="#myPictures"
        data-bs-slide="next"
      >
        <span className="carousel-control-next-icon" aria-hidden="true"></span>
        <span className="visually-hidden">Next</span>
      </button>
    </div>
  );
}

        <a className="navbar-brand" href="#">
          Navbar
        </a>
        <button
          className="navbar-toggler"
          type="button"
          data-bs-toggle="collapse"
          data-bs-target="#navbarNavAltMarkup"
          aria-controls="navbarNavAltMarkup"
          aria-expanded="false"
          aria-label="Toggle navigation"
        >
          <span className="navbar-toggler-icon"></span>
        </button>
        <div className="collapse navbar-collapse" id="navbarNavAltMarkup">
          <div className="navbar-nav">
            <NavLink className="nav-link" aria-current="page" to="/">
              Home
            </NavLink>
            <NavLink className="nav-link" to="/videos">
              Videos
            </NavLink>
            <NavLink className="nav-link" to="/responsive">
              Responsive
            </NavLink>
            <a className="nav-link disabled" aria-disabled="true">
              Disabled
            </a>
            <SignInArea />
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </nav>
  );
}

///// FILE: "React/src/Views/Modal.js"

import React from "react";

export function Modal() {
  return (
    <>
      <button
        type="button"
        className="btn btn-primary"
        data-bs-toggle="modal"
        data-bs-target="#exampleModal"
      >
        Launch Bootstrap modal
      </button>

      <div
        className="modal fade"
        id="exampleModal"
        tabIndex="-1"
        aria-labelledby="exampleModalLabel"
        aria-hidden="true"
      >
        <div className="modal-dialog">
          <div className="modal-content">
            <div className="modal-header">
              <h1 className="modal-title fs-5" id="exampleModalLabel">
                Modal title
              </h1>
              <button
                type="button"
                className="btn-close"
                data-bs-dismiss="modal"
                aria-label="Close"
              ></button>
            </div>
            <div className="modal-body">This is a Bootstrap modal!!!</div>
            <div className="modal-footer">
              <button
                type="button"
                className="btn btn-secondary"
                data-bs-dismiss="modal"
              >
                Close
              </button>
              <button type="button" className="btn btn-primary">
                Save changes
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </>
  );
}


///// FILE: "React/src/Views/MyGreeting.js"

import React, { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { Link } from "react-router";

export function MyGreeting() {
  debugger;

  const [greeting, setGreeting] = useState("Amazing world!");
  const [didMount, setDidMount] = useState(false);

  // const myTuple = useState("Amazing world!");
  // const greeting = myTuple[0];
  // const setGreeting = myTuple[1];

  useEffect(componentDidMount, []);
  useEffect(componentDidUpdate, [greeting]);
  useEffect(componentDidUnmount, []);

  return (
    <>
      <header>
        <nav>
          <Link to="/">HOME | </Link>
          <Link>ABOUT | </Link>
          <Link>CONTACT | </Link>
          <Link>GALLERY | </Link>
          <Link to="/greeting">GREETING | </Link>
          <Link to="/videos">VIDEOS</Link>
        </nav>
      </header>
      <main>
        <h3>My Greeting</h3>
        <p>{greeting}</p>
      </main>
    </>
  );

  function changeGreeting() {
    setGreeting("Have a nice day!");
  }

  function componentDidMount() {
    debugger;
    setDidMount(true);
    console.log("The component mounted. The greeting is " + greeting);
    setTimeout(changeGreeting, 3000);
  }
  function componentDidUpdate() {
    debugger;
    // console.log("The component mounted or updated.");

    if (didMount)
      console.log("The component updated. The greeting is " + greeting);
  }

  function componentDidUnmount() {
    debugger;
    return function () {
      debugger;
      console.log("component did unmount");
    };
  }
}


///// FILE: "React/src/Views/Navbar.js"

import React from "react";
import { Link, NavLink } from "react-router";

/**************************************************
 * <Link> was replaced by <NavLink>
 * <NavLink> automatically adds the active class
 ***************************************************/

export function Navbar() {
  const domain = window.location.hostname;
  let rootPath = "";
  if (domain === "rolazar.github.io") rootPath = "/react-navigation";
  console.log(`The domain is ${domain}`);

  return (
    <nav className="nav nav-pills">
      <NavLink className="nav-link" to={`${rootPath}/`}>
        HOME
      </NavLink>
      {/* <NavLink className="nav-link">ABOUT</NavLink> */}
      {/* <NavLink className="nav-link highlight">CONTACT</NavLink> */}
      {/* <NavLink className="nav-link">GALLERY</NavLink> */}
      <NavLink className="nav-link" to={`${rootPath}/greeting`}>
        GREETING
      </NavLink>
      <NavLink className="nav-link" to={`${rootPath}/videos`}>
        VIDEOS
      </NavLink>
      <NavLink className="nav-link" to="/responsive">
        RESPONSIVE
      </NavLink>
    </nav>
  );
}


///// FILE: "React/src/Views/OutputPractice.js"

import React, { useState } from "react";

export function OutputPractice() {
  debugger;
  const [message, setMessage] = useState(
    <p>Hello OutputPractice component!</p>
  );
  return (
    <main>
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
        Enter some text:
        <input />
        <input type="submit" />
      </form>
      <output>{message}</output>
    </main>
  );

  function handleSubmit(event = new Event()) {
    debugger;

    event.preventDefault();
    const inputs = event.target;
    const textInput = inputs[0];
    const userText = textInput.value;
    setMessage(
      <>
        {message}
        <p>You entered {userText}</p>
      </>
    );
  }
}

///// FILE: "React/src/Views/SignInArea.js"

import React, { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { SignInModal } from "./SignInModal";
import { SignOutModal } from "./SignOutModal";

export function SignInArea() {
  const [button, setButton] = useState(<></>);
  const [isSignedIn, setIsSignedIn] = useState(false);
  const [didMount, setDidMount] = useState(false);

  useEffect(componentDidMount, []);
  useEffect(componentDidUpdate, [isSignedIn]);

  return <>{button}</>;

  function componentDidMount() {
    console.log("MOUNT PHASE: SignInArea");
    setDidMount(true);

    if (isSignedIn) setButton(<SignOutModal onSignOut={handleSignOut} />);
    else setButton(<SignInModal onSignIn={handleSignIn} />);
  }

  function componentDidUpdate() {
    if (didMount) {
      console.log("UPDATE PHASE: SignInArea");
      if (isSignedIn) setButton(<SignOutModal onSignOut={handleSignOut} />);
      else setButton(<SignInModal onSignIn={handleSignIn} />);
    }
  }

  function handleSignIn() {
    setIsSignedIn(true);
  }

  function handleSignOut() {
    setIsSignedIn(false);
  }
}


///// FILE: "React/src/Views/SignInContent.js"

import React from "react";

export function SignInContent(props) {
  const errorMessage = props.errorMessage;

  return (
    <>
      Email: <input type="email" required />
      <br />
      Password: <input type="password" required />
      <div style={{ color: "red" }}>{errorMessage}</div>
    </>
  );
}


///// FILE: "React/src/Views/SignInModal.js"

import React, { useState } from "react";
import { SignInContent } from "./SignInContent";
import { handleSignInAttempt } from "../controllers/handleSignInAttempt";

export function SignInModal(props) {
  const onSignIn = props.onSignIn;
  const [errorMessage, setErrorMessage] = useState("");
  return (
    <>
      <button
        type="button"
        className="btn btn-secondary"
        data-bs-toggle="modal"
        data-bs-target="#signInModal"
      >
        Sign In
      </button>

      <form
        onSubmit={handleSubmit}
        className="modal fade"
        id="signInModal"
        tabIndex="-1"
        aria-labelledby="signInModalLabel"
        aria-hidden="true"
      >
        <div className="modal-dialog">
          <div className="modal-content">
            <div className="modal-header">
              <h1 className="modal-title fs-5" id="signInModalLabel">
                Sign In
              </h1>
              <button
                type="button"
                className="btn-close"
                data-bs-dismiss="modal"
                aria-label="Close"
              ></button>
            </div>
            <div className="modal-body">
              <SignInContent errorMessage={errorMessage} />
            </div>
            <div className="modal-footer">
              <button
                type="button"
                className="btn btn-secondary"
                data-bs-dismiss="modal"
              >
                Close
              </button>
              <button type="submit" className="btn btn-primary">
                Sign In
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </form>
    </>
  );

  function handleSubmit(event) {
    const errorMessage = handleSignInAttempt(event);
    if (errorMessage) setErrorMessage(errorMessage);
    else onSignIn();
  }
}


///// FILE: "React/src/Views/SignOutModal.js"

import React from "react";

export function SignOutModal(props) {
  const onSignOut = props.onSignOut;

  return (
    <>
      <button
        type="button"
        className="btn btn-secondary"
        data-bs-toggle="modal"
        data-bs-target="#signOutModal"
      >
        Sign Out
      </button>

      <form
        onSubmit={handleSubmit}
        className="modal fade"
        id="signOutModal"
        tabIndex="-1"
        aria-labelledby="signOutModalLabel"
        aria-hidden="true"
      >
        <div className="modal-dialog">
          <div className="modal-content">
            <div className="modal-header">
              <h1 className="modal-title fs-5" id="signOutModalLabel">
                Sign Out
              </h1>
              <button
                type="button"
                className="btn-close"
                data-bs-dismiss="modal"
                aria-label="Close"
              ></button>
            </div>
            <div className="modal-body">Are you sure you want to sign out?</div>
            <div className="modal-footer">
              <button
                type="button"
                className="btn btn-secondary"
                data-bs-dismiss="modal"
              >
                Close
              </button>
              <button type="submit" className="btn btn-primary">
                Sign Out
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </form>
    </>
  );

  function handleSubmit(event = new Event()) {
    event.preventDefault();
    const inputs = event.target;
    const closeButton = inputs[1];
    closeButton.click();
    onSignOut();
  }
}


///// FILE: "React/src/Views/Twitch.js"

import React from "react";
import "../index.scss";

export function Twitch(props) {
  const src = props.src;
  const label = props.label;
  const captions = props.children;
  // const center = { width: "fit-content", justifySelf: "center" };
  // const depth = { borderRadius: "10px", boxShadow: "10px 10px grey" };

  return (
    <div
      className="center"
      // style={center}
    >
      <h3>{label}</h3>
      <p>{captions}</p>
      <iframe
        className="depth"
        src={src}
        frameBorder="0"
        allowFullScreen={true}
        scrolling="no"
        height="378"
        width="620"
        // style={depth}
      ></iframe>
    </div>
  );
}

import React from "react";

export function Video(props) {
  const src = props.src;
  const label = props.label;
  const captions = props.children;
  return (
    <>
      <h3>{label}</h3>
      <p>{captions}</p>
      <video src={src} width="500px" controls></video>
    </>
  );
}

  );

  useEffect(componentDidMount, []);

  return (
    <main id="videos">

///// FILE: "React/src/Views/Vimeo.js"

import React from "react";

export function Vimeo(props) {
  const src = props.src;
  const label = props.label;
  const captions = props.children;
  return (
    <>
      <h3>{label}</h3>
      <p>{captions}</p>
      <div
        style={{
          padding: "56.25% 0 0 0",
          position: "relative",
        }}
      >
        <iframe
          src={src}
          frameBorder="0"
          allow="autoplay; fullscreen; picture-in-picture; clipboard-write"
          style={{
            position: "absolute",
            top: 0,
            left: 0,
            width: "100%",
            height: "100%",
          }}
          title="christmas."
        ></iframe>
      </div>
      <script src="https://player.vimeo.com/api/player.js"></script>
    </>
  );
}


///// FILE: "React/src/Views/YouTube.js"

import React, { useEffect } from "react";

export function YouTube(props) {
  const src = props.src;
  const label = props.label;
  const captions = props.children;
  const dimensions = {
    width: "100vw",
    height: "56.25vw",
  };

  useEffect(componentDidUnmount, []);

  return (
    <>
      <h3>{label}</h3>
      <p>{captions}</p>
      <div style={dimensions}>
        <iframe
          // width="560"
          // height="315"
          width="100%"
          height="100%"
          src={src}
          title="YouTube video player"
          frameBorder="0"
          allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share"
          referrerPolicy="strict-origin-when-cross-origin"
          allowFullScreen
        ></iframe>
      </div>
    </>
  );

  function componentDidUnmount() {
    return function () {
      console.log("YouTube component unmounted.");
    };
  }
}

///// FILE: "React/testing.md"

# Testing

### Unit Testing

- Individual functions or classes are tested to ensure they work as expected
- Automatically check functions or classes for bugs
- Describe what is being tested and how to test it

### Describe a test

`const result = addition(x, y);`

- What is being tested? The addition function
- What is expected? The result to be the addition of x and y
- How to prepare the test? Set the numerical values of x and y

### Jest

- A node module (or package) for writing automated tests

1. npm install jest
2. npm install @jest/globals

### Babel

- A node module (or package) for converting export/import syntax to the old way
- Jest is only compatible with the old import/export syntax

1. npm install @babel/core
2. npm install @babel/preset-env
3. Add to `babel.config.json` “presets”: [“@babel/preset-env”]

### Write a test description

`test("The addition function adds numbers", callbackTest1);`

1. Code the `addition` function in `addition.js`
2. Create `addition.test.js` and import the `addition` function
3. Use the `test` function to describe the test
4. Include a callback which will contain instructions for the test

### AAA test phases

- Instructions for a unit test should include AAA phases
- A unit is the function or class being tested

1. Arrange – Set the variables for the test
2. Act – Use the unit with the variables
3. Assert – Check if the unit works as expected

### Write the test with AAA phases

1. Arrange – In the callback, set the numerical values of `x` and `y`
2. Act – Use the `addition` function with the variables and capture the `result`
3. Assert – Use the `expect` function and the `toBe` method to validate the result
4. Use comments to mark each test phase

### Run the automated test

- The Jest module searches for test files and runs the tests they contain

1. In the terminal, `npx jest`
2. Observe the results

### Add another test

`test("The addition function adds a positive and negative number", callbackTest2);`

- Write a test in `addition.test.js` using `addition` with a positive and negative number

1. Use the `test` function to describe what is being tested and include `callbackTest2`
2. Write the test instructions in `callbackTest2`
3. Include AAA phases in the test and use comments to mark each phase
4. Use Jest to run the tests

### Group the tests together

`describe("Test the addition function", function () {} );`

- Tests can be grouped together with the `describe` function and an anonymous function

1. Use the `describe` function to indicate that the `addition` function is being tested
2. Move the tests into the anonymous function code block
3. Rewrite the test descriptions to be less redundant
4. Use Jest to run the tests and observe the difference

### Arrow function

```javascript
function () {};
() => {};
```

- An arrow function can take the place of an anonymous function

1. Remove the function keyword
2. Put an arrow between the parentheses and the code block

### Increase readability

`describe("Test the addition function", () => {} );`

- Use an arrow function and the it function to increase readability

1. Replace the anonymous function with an arrow function
2. Replace the `test` function with the `it` function
3. Rewrite the test descriptions to be less redundant
4. Rename the callbacks to describe what they are testing

### Test more possibilities

`it("adds negative numbers", addNegatives);`

- Write a test for the addition function with 2 negative numbers

1. Use the `it` function to describe the test and include a descriptive callback
2. Write the test instructions in the callback
3. Include AAA phases in the test and use comments to mark each phase
4. Use Jest to run the tests

### Test unlikely possibilities

`expect(result).toBe(NaN);`

1. Test when the variables are strings
2. Test when the variables are number strings
3. Use Jest to run the tests

### Failed tests

`const result = Number(x) + Number(y);`

- When a test fails, find out what went wrong

1. Check the test for bugs
2. Check the addition function for bugs
3. Change the addition function to handle strings
4. Use Jest to run the tests

### Unit Testing Summary

- jest package
- @jest/lobals package
- @babel/core
- @babel/preset-env
- `describe` function
- `test` function
- `it` function
- `expect` function
- Filename with .test.js
- Test likely possibilities
- Test unlikely possibilities
- Arrange phase
- Act phase
- Assert phase

### Test DatabaseSimulation

1. Use the `describe` function for the constructor
2. Add tests for likely and unlikely possibilities
3. Use the `describe` function for `getData`
4. Add tests for likely and unlikely possibilities
5. Use Jest to run the tests

### Integration testing

- A set of functions or classes are tested to ensure they work together
- Because one unit depends on another unit, the test results may not be reliable
- The inner unit should be thoroughly tested and in working order

### Test authenticationSimulationDB

1. Test when the email and password are correct
2. Test when the email is correct, and password is incorrect
3. Test when the email is not in the list
4. Test when the email is in the list, but the password is empty
5. Test when the email is empty, but the password is in the list

### toBe vs toEqual

```javascript
expect(result).toBe("dog");
expect(result).toEqual({ animal: "dog" });
```

- Use `toBe` for strings, numbers, Booleans, NaN, null, and undefined
- Use `toEqual` for objects, arrays, classes, and functions
- Other expect methods https://jestjs.io/docs/expect

### Test Driven Development

- The technique of writing tests first, then writing the code afterwards
- The tests act like a todo list, and can help with code planning and design
- As tests pass, they provide a sense of achievement and satisfaction
- TDD can reduce the feeling of being overwhelmed because each test is a small step

### Functional Programming

- The technique of writing functions that accept input values and return output values
- Code is more readable because functions describe what they do
- Code is more reusable, especially if the functions accomplish only 1 task
- Code is more composable — small functions can be combined to create a large function

### TDD and Functional Programming

- Combine Test Driven Development and functional programming
- Tests will be easier to write
- Code will be faster to develop


///// FILE: "React/vscode.md"

# VS Code

### Automatic code formatting and indentation

- Prettier can automatically format code, but it may require manual configuration

1. Open a new VS Code window (without a project)
2. Access the global settings file
3. Add `"editor.defaultFormatter": "esbenp.prettier-vscode",`
4. Add `"editor.formatOnSave": true,`

### Debug with VS Code instead of Dev Tools

1. Open a new VS Code window (without a project) to access global settings
2. Menu → Run → Add Configuration → `Chrome: Launch`
3. Change the `name` to “VS Code Debugger”
4. Change the `url` to your server
5. Disable Live Server from automatically opening a browser

### VS Code OCR app

1. View the article https://devpost.com/software/web-based-clipboard-ocr
2. Try the online OCR app (link at the bottom of the article)
3. Copy the app to a VS Code project
4. Run the OCR app locally

export default {
  //MODULES ARE FILES THAT ARE IMPORTED
  module: {
    //RULES ARE A LIST OF WAYS TO PROCESS THE MODULES
    rules: [
      {
        exclude: /\.(scss|css|otf|ttf|json)/, //DON'T COMPILE STYLE MODULES
        test: /\.js/, //COMPILE JAVASCRIPT MODULES
        use: "babel-loader", //USE THIS LOADER TO COMPILE ALL OTHER MODULES
      },
      {
        test: /\.(scss|css)/, //COMPILE STYLE MODULES
        use: ["style-loader", "css-loader", "sass-loader"], //USE THESE LOADERS TO COMPILE STYLE MODULES
      },
      {
        test: /\.(jpg|png|mp4)/, //EXAMINE ASSET FILES
        type: "asset/resource", //SPECIFY THAT THESE FILES ARE ASSETS OR RESOURCE. USE THIS BUILT-IN FEATURE TO HANDLE ASSETS.
      },
    ],
  },
  watch: true, //WATCH FOR CODE CHANGES. PRESS CTRL+C TO CANCEL
  watchOptions: { aggregateTimeout: 2000 }, //GIVE WEBPACK MORE TIME TO COMPILE
  mode: "development", //ENABLES THE DEBUGGER
  devtool: "source-map", //ENABLES DEBUGGER CODE TO MATCH ACTUAL CODE
};

///// FILE: "React Template/redirect.js"

/**************************************************************
 * @summary Redirects the SPA to the root path
 * @param rootPath Set this to the correct root path
 * @description
 * Useful when an SPA page is refreshed.
 * Load this module through 404.html to redirect on 404 errors.
 * By redirecting to the root path, 404 errors are removed.
 * Use Redirect.js to redirect to the path where the 404 occured.
 **************************************************************/

const rootPath = "/react-navigation";
const path = window.location.pathname;
window.localStorage.setItem("redirect", path);
window.location.replace(rootPath);




///// FILE: "React Template/src/index.js"

import { createRoot } from "react-dom/client";
import React from "react";
import { Home } from "./Views/Home";
import { BrowserRouter, Route, Routes } from "react-router";
import { Contact } from "./Views/Contact";
import { About } from "./Views/About";
import { HandleRefresh } from "./Views/HandleRefresh";
import { rootPath } from "./utils/rootPath";
import { Custom404 } from "./Views/Custom404";

const root = createRoot(window.bodyTag);
root.render(
  <BrowserRouter>
    <HandleRefresh>
      <Routes>
        <Route path={`${rootPath}/`} element={<Home />} />
        <Route path={`${rootPath}/contact`} element={<Contact />} />
        <Route path={`${rootPath}/about`} element={<About />} />
        <Route path="*" element={<Custom404 />} />
      </Routes>
    </HandleRefresh>
  </BrowserRouter>
);


///// FILE: "React Template/src/utils/output.js"

export function output(
  message = "",
  outputTag = "outputTag",
  shouldAppend = true
) {
  if (shouldAppend) window[outputTag].innerHTML += message;
  else window[outputTag].innerHTML = message;
}

///// FILE: "React Template/src/Views/HandleRefresh.js"

import React, { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router";

/*************************************************
 * @summary Removes the 404 error on SPA refresh
 * @param props.children The elements to render on refresh
 * @description
 * This component depends on the local storage used by redirect.js
 * In redirect.js, properly set the root path.
 */
export function HandleRefresh(props) {
  const children = props.children;
  const navigateTo = useNavigate();
  const [didMount, setDidMount] = useState(false);
  useEffect(componentDidMount, []);

  if (didMount) return <>{children}</>;
  else return <></>;

  function componentDidMount() {
    const redirectPath = localStorage.getItem("redirect");
    if (redirectPath) {
      navigateTo(redirectPath);
      localStorage.setItem("redirect", "");
      setTimeout(() => setDidMount(true), 1000);
    } else setDidMount(true);
  }
}

///// FILE: "React Practice/src/controllers/handleSubmit.js"

import { output } from "../utils/output";
import { Trivia } from "../utils/Trivia";

export function handleSubmit(event = new Event()) {
  event.preventDefault();
  const inputs = event.target;
  const options = inputs[0];
  const multiple = options[0];
  const boolean = options[1];
  const number = inputs[1];

  output(`Value of multiple is ${multiple.value}<br>`, "myTag");
  output(`Is multiple selected? ${multiple.selected}<br>`, "myTag");

  output(`Value of boolean is ${boolean.value}<br>`, "myTag");
  output(`Is boolean selected? ${boolean.selected}<br>`, "myTag");

  const trivia = new Trivia();
  trivia.amount = number.value;

  if (multiple.selected) trivia.type = multiple.value;
  if (boolean.selected) trivia.type = boolean.value;

  const baseURL = "http://opentdb.com/api.php";
  const corsProxy = "https://corsproxy.io/?url=";
  const thingProxy = "https://thingproxy.freeboard.io/fetch/";
  const url = `${thingProxy}${baseURL}?amount=${trivia.amount}&type=${trivia.type}`;
  debugger;

  const promise = fetch(url);
  promise.then(getServerResponse);
  debugger;
}

function getServerResponse(response = new Response()) {
  const promise = response.text();
  promise.then(getJsonString);
  debugger;
}

function getJsonString(stringifiedObject = "") {
  const opentdbObject = JSON.parse(stringifiedObject);
  const triviaQuestions = opentdbObject.results;
  const triviaDetails = triviaQuestions[0];
  const question = triviaDetails.question;
  const correctAnswer = triviaDetails.correct_answer;
  const incorrectAnswers = triviaDetails.incorrect_answers;

  console.log(opentdbObject);

  output(`<br>${question}<br>`, "myTag");
  output(`A. ${correctAnswer}<br>`, "myTag");
  output(`B. ${incorrectAnswers[0]}<br>`, "myTag");
  output(`C. ${incorrectAnswers[1]}<br>`, "myTag");
  output(`D. ${incorrectAnswers[2]}<br>`, "myTag");
  debugger;
}

///// FILE: "React Practice/src/utils/output.js"

export function output(
  message = "",
  outputTag = "outputTag",
  shouldAppend = true
) {
  debugger;
  const outputElement = document.getElementById(outputTag);
  if (shouldAppend) outputElement.innerHTML += message;
  else outputElement.innerHTML = message;
  debugger;
}


///// FILE: "React Practice/src/utils/Trivia.js"

export class Trivia {
  amount = 1;
  type = "";
}


///// FILE: "React Practice/src/Views/ReactPractice.js"

import React from "react";
import { handleSubmit } from "../controllers/handleSubmit";

export function ReactPractice() {
  return (
    <>
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
        <div>
          What type of trivia questions do you want?
          <br />
          <select title="dropdown">
            <option>multiple</option>
            <option>boolean</option>
          </select>
        </div>
        <div>
          How many trivia questions do you want?
          <br />
          <input type="number" defaultValue="1" min="1" max="3" />
          <br />
        </div>
        <input type="submit" />
      </form>
      <output id="myTag"></output>
    </>
  );
}

/* Tesseract.js https://github.com/naptha/tesseract.js#tesseractjs */

var lang = "eng";
var blob;
var currZoom;
var draggingElement;

function PopulateSelects() {
  var languageSelect = document.getElementById("language");
  for (var name in languagesList) {
    languageSelect.innerHTML +=
      "<option value='" +
      name +
      "'>" +
      name +
      " (" +
      languagesList[name] +
      ")" +
      "</option>";
  }
  language.value = "English";
  lang = "eng";
}
function setLanguage() {
  var languageSelect = document.getElementById("language");
  lang = languagesList[languageSelect.value];
  console.log(lang);
}

function resetImage() {
  pastedImage = document.getElementById("pastedImage");
  if (pastedImage) {
    currZoom = pastedImage.naturalWidth;
    pastedImage.style.width = currZoom + "px";
    pastedImage.style.removeProperty("width");
    pastedImage.style.removeProperty("left");
    pastedImage.style.removeProperty("top");
  }
}

function tesseract(blob) {
  var reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = function (event) {
    document.getElementById("Output").value = "Working....";
    console.log(event.target.result); // clipboard image data url!
    Tesseract.recognize(blob, lang, {
      logger: (m) => {
        /* if ( m.progress != 1 )*/ // eng=english, fra=french
        document.getElementById("Output").value =
          m.status + " " + (m.progress * 100).toFixed(0) + "%";
        console.log(m);
      },
    }).then(({ data: { text } }) => {
      document.getElementById("Output").value = text;
    });
    //console.log(event.target.result)

    pastedImage = document.getElementById("pastedImage");
    pastedImage.style.removeProperty("display");
    pastedImage.style.removeProperty("width");
    pastedImage.style.removeProperty("left");
    pastedImage.style.removeProperty("top");

    document.getElementById("pastedImage").src = event.target.result;
  };
  reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
}
document.body.onpaste = function (event) {
  // use event.originalEvent.clipboard for newer chrome versions
  var items = (event.clipboardData || event.originalEvent.clipboardData).items;
  console.log(JSON.stringify(items)); // will give you the mime types
  // find pasted image among pasted items
  var blob = null;
  for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
    if (items[i].type.indexOf("image") === 0) {
      blob = items[i].getAsFile();
    }
  }
  // load image if there is a pasted image
  if (blob !== null) {
    tesseract(blob);
  }
};

document.body.addEventListener("drop", function (e) {
  e.stopPropagation();
  e.preventDefault();
  var items = e.dataTransfer.items; // Array of all files
  var blob = null;
  for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
    if (items[i].type.indexOf("image") === 0) {
      blob = items[i].getAsFile();
    }
  }
  if (blob !== null) {
    tesseract(blob);
  }
});

function resizeWindow() {
  outputHolder = document.getElementById("outputHolder");
  // if (window.innerHeight >= 400)

  // }
}

function copyOutput() {
  output = document.getElementById("Output");
  output.select();
  output.setSelectionRange(0, 99999); /* For mobile devices */

  /* Copy the text inside the text field */
  document.execCommand("copy");
}
function cleanBlankLines() {
  output = document.getElementById("Output");
  output.value = output.value.replaceAll(/(\n)+/g, "\n");
}
function clearOutput() {
  document.getElementById("Output").value = "";
}

var coordX;
var coordY;

function startDrag(e) {
  // determine event object
  if (!e) {
    var e = window.event;
  }

  // IE uses srcElement, others use target
  var targ = e.target ? e.target : e.srcElement;
  if (targ.className != "draggable") {
    return;
  }
  draggingElement = targ;

  // calculate event X, Y coordinates
  offsetX = e.clientX;
  offsetY = e.clientY;

  // assign default values for top and left properties
  if (!targ.style.left) {
    targ.style.left = targ.offsetLeft;
  }
  if (!targ.style.top) {
    targ.style.top = targ.offsetTop;
  }

  // calculate integer values for top and left
  // properties
  coordX = parseInt(targ.offsetLeft);
  coordY = parseInt(targ.offsetTop);
  drag = true;

  // move div element
  document.onmousemove = dragDiv;

  return false;
}

function dragDiv(e) {
  if (!drag) {
    return;
  }
  if (!e) {
    var e = window.event;
  }
  var targ = e.target ? e.target : e.srcElement;
  targ = draggingElement;
  // move div element
  // if(coordX + e.clientX - offsetX > 0)
  targ.style.left = coordX + e.clientX - offsetX + "px";
  // if(coordY + e.clientY - offsetY > 0)
  targ.style.top = coordY + e.clientY - offsetY + "px";
  return false;
}

function zoomImage(event) {
  if (!e) {
    var e = window.event;
  }

  var targ = e.target ? e.target : e.srcElement;
  if (!draggingElement) {
    if (targ.className != "draggable") {
      return;
    }
    draggingElement = targ;
  }
  if (!targ || targ.className != "draggable") return;
  // targ = draggingElement;

  // move div element
  if (!currZoom) {
    currZoom = targ.naturalWidth;
  }
  currZoom = currZoom - event.deltaY;
  // if (currZoom > 1500)
  //     currZoom = 1500;
  if (currZoom < 100) {
    currZoom = currZoom + event.deltaY;
    return;
  }

  if (!targ.style.left) {
    targ.style.left = targ.offsetLeft;
  }
  if (!targ.style.top) {
    targ.style.top = targ.offsetTop;
  }

  console.log((e.clientX - targ.offsetLeft) / targ.width);
  console.log(parseInt(targ.style.top) + "//" + targ.scrollHeight);

  targ.style.width = currZoom + "px";
  targ.style.top =
    targ.offsetTop +
    (targ.height / targ.width) *
      ((e.clientY - targ.offsetTop) / targ.height) *
      event.deltaY +
    "px";
  targ.style.left =
    targ.offsetLeft +
    ((e.clientX - targ.offsetLeft) / targ.width) * event.deltaY +
    "px";
}

function stopDrag() {
  drag = false;
}

var alignedTop = false;
function swapVertPosition() {
  if (alignedTop) {
    document.documentElement.style.removeProperty("--top");
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty("--bottom", "0px");
    alignedTop = false;
  } else {
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty("--top", "41px");
    document.documentElement.style.removeProperty("--bottom");
    alignedTop = true;
  }
}

var alignedLeft = false;
function swapHorPosition() {
  if (alignedLeft) {
    document.documentElement.style.removeProperty("--left");
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty("--right", "0px");
    alignedLeft = false;
  } else {
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty("--left", "0px");
    document.documentElement.style.removeProperty("--right");
    alignedLeft = true;
  }
}

window.onload = function () {
  resizeWindow();
  document.body.addEventListener("resize", resizeWindow, false);
  PopulateSelects();
  document
    .getElementById("language")
    .addEventListener("change", setLanguage, false);

  document.onmousedown = startDrag;
  document.onmouseup = stopDrag;
  document.onwheel = zoomImage;

  document
    .getElementById("resetImage")
    .addEventListener("click", resetImage, false);

  document
    .getElementById("copyOutput")
    .addEventListener("click", copyOutput, false);
  document
    .getElementById("cleanBlankLines")
    .addEventListener("click", cleanBlankLines, false);
  document
    .getElementById("clearOutput")
    .addEventListener("click", clearOutput, false);

  document
    .getElementById("updown")
    .addEventListener("click", swapVertPosition, false);
  document
    .getElementById("leftright")
    .addEventListener("click", swapHorPosition, false);
};

function practice1() {
  debugger;

  const object = {
    property1: "I'm a string",
    property2: 2024,
    property3: false,
  };

  output(`property1 is ${object.property1}<br>`);
  output(`property2 is ${object.property2}<br>`);
  output(`property3 is ${object.property3}<br>`);
}

function practice2() {
  debugger;

  const myArray = [];
  myArray.push("I'm a string");
  myArray.push(2024);
  myArray.push(false);

  const count = myArray.length;
  for (let position = 0; position < count; position++) {
    const value = myArray[position];
    output(`The value at position ${position} is ${value}<br>`);
  }
}

function practice3() {
  debugger;

  const car1 = {
    color: "red",
    year: 2022,
    forSale: false,
  };

  const car2 = {
    color: "black",
    year: 2023,
    forSale: true,
  };

  const car3 = {
    color: "red",
    year: 2024,
    forSale: false,
  };

  const myCars = [];
  myCars.push(car1);
  myCars.push(car2);
  myCars.push(car3);

  const count = myCars.length;
  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const car = myCars[i];
    const color = car.color;
    const year = car.year;
    const forSale = car.forSale;
    const carNumber = i + 1;

    output(`Car number ${carNumber} properties:<br>`);
    output(`The color is ${color}<br>`);
    output(`The year is ${year}<br>`);
    output(`Is the car for sale? ${forSale}<br><br>`);
  }
}

function practice1() {
  debugger;

  const myObject = {
    property1: ["Hello world!", 2024, true],
  };
  const myArray = myObject.property1;
  output(myArray[0] + "<br>");
  output(myArray[1] + "<br>");
  output(myArray[2] + "<br>");
}

function practice2() {
  debugger;

  const myObject = {
    property1: ["hello", 123, true],
    property2: ["hi", 2024, false],
    property3: ["farewell", 111, true],
  };

  const myArray1 = myObject.property1;
  const myArray2 = myObject.property2;
  const myArray3 = myObject.property3;

  for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
    const array1Item = myArray1[i];
    const array2Item = myArray2[i];
    const array3Item = myArray3[i];
    output(`${array1Item} ${array2Item} ${array3Item}<br>`, "outputTag2");
  }
}

function practice3() {
  debugger;

  const myObject = {
    property1: ["hello", 123, true],
    property2: ["hi", 2024, false],
    property3: ["farewell", 111, true],
  };

  for (let propertyNumber = 1; propertyNumber <= 3; propertyNumber++) {
    const propertyName = `property${propertyNumber}`;
    const array = myObject[propertyName];
    const myString = array[0];
    const myNumber = array[1];
    const myBoolean = array[2];
    output(`${myString} ${myNumber} ${myBoolean}<br>`, "outputTag3");
  }
}

function practice4() {
  debugger;

  const myObject = {
    propertyOne: ["hello", 123, true],
    propertyTwo: ["hi", 2024, false],
    propertyThree: ["farewell", 111, true],
  };

  for (let propertyName in myObject) {
    const myArray = myObject[propertyName];
    output(`${propertyName} contains `, "outputTag4");

    for (let item of myArray) {
      output(`${item} `, "outputTag4");
    }

    output("<br>", "outputTag4");
  }
}

class Column {
  openingTag = "<div class='col'>";
  closingTag = "</div>";
  innerHTML = "";

  constructor(content = "") {
    this.innerHTML = content;
  }

  toString() {
    return `${this.openingTag}${this.innerHTML}${this.closingTag}`;
  }

  info(columnNumber) {
    console.log("The column number is " + columnNumber);
  }

  content() {
    console.log("The content is: " + this.innerHTML);
  }
}

function practice1() {
  debugger;

  const gridSystem = `
    <div class="container">
        <div class="row">
          <div class="col">COLUMN 1</div>
          <div class="col">COLUMN 2</div>
          <div class="col">COLUMN 3</div>
        </div>
    </div>`;
  output(gridSystem);
}

function practice2() {
  debugger;

  let columns = "";
  for (let columnNumber = 1; columnNumber <= 3; columnNumber++) {
    columns += `<div class="col">COLUMN ${columnNumber}</div>`;
  }

  const gridSystem = `
          <div class="container">
              <div class="row">
                ${columns}
            </div>
          </div>`;

  output(gridSystem, "outputTag2");
}

function practice3() {
  debugger;

  let rows = "";
  for (let rowNumber = 1; rowNumber <= 3; rowNumber++) {
    let columns = "";
    for (let columnNumber = 1; columnNumber <= 3; columnNumber++) {
      columns += `<div class="col">COLUMN ${columnNumber}</div>`;
    }

    rows += `<div class="row">${columns}</div>`;
  }

  const gridSystem = `
          <div class="container">
              ${rows}
          </div>`;

  output(gridSystem, "outputTag3");
}

function practice4() {
  debugger;

  let rows = "";
  for (let rowNumber = 1; rowNumber <= 3; rowNumber++) {
    let columns = "";
    for (let columnNumber = 1; columnNumber <= 3; columnNumber++) {
      const column = new Column();
      column.info(columnNumber);
      column.innerHTML = `COLUMN ${columnNumber}`;
      column.content();
      columns += `${column.openingTag}${column.innerHTML}${column.closingTag}`;
    }

    rows += `<div class="row">${columns}</div>`;
  }

  const gridSystem = `
          <div class="container">
              ${rows}
          </div>`;

  output(gridSystem, "outputTag4");
}

function practice5() {
  debugger;

  let rows = "";
  for (let rowNumber = 1; rowNumber <= 3; rowNumber++) {
    let columns = "";
    for (let columnNumber = 1; columnNumber <= 3; columnNumber++) {
      const column = new Column(`COLUMN ${columnNumber}`);
      columns += column;
    }

    rows += `<div class="row">${columns}</div>`;
  }

  const gridSystem = `
          <div class="container">
              ${rows}
          </div>`;

  output(gridSystem, "outputTag5");
}

///// FILE: "Practice Level 2/day4.js"

function handleSubmit(event = new Event()) {
  debugger;
  event.preventDefault();

  const inputs = event.target;

  const redInput = inputs[0];
  const whiteInput = inputs[1];
  const blueInput = inputs[2];
  const yellowInput = inputs[3];

  const redChecked = redInput.checked;
  const whiteChecked = whiteInput.checked;
  const blueChecked = blueInput.checked;
  const yellowChecked = yellowInput.checked;

  output(`redChecked: ${redChecked}<br>`);
  output(`whiteChecked: ${whiteChecked}<br>`);
  output(`blueChecked: ${blueChecked}<br>`);
  output(`yellowChecked: ${yellowChecked}<br>`);

  const count = inputs.length;
  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const radioInput = inputs[i];
    const name = radioInput.name;
    output(`${name}<br>`);
  }

  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const radioInput = inputs[i];
    const value = radioInput.value;
    output(`${value}<br>`);
  }

  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const radioInput = inputs[i];
    const value = radioInput.value;
    const isChecked = radioInput.checked;
    if (isChecked) output(`${value}<br>`);
  }

  output("<br>The checked data type is ");
  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const radioInput = inputs[i];
    const value = radioInput.value;
    const name = radioInput.name;
    const isChecked = radioInput.checked;
    const isDataType = name === "dataType";
    if (isChecked && isDataType) output(`${value}<br>`);
  }
}

///// FILE: "Practice Level 2/utility-functions.js"

function output(message = "", outputTag = "outputTag", shouldAppend = true) {
  if (shouldAppend) window[outputTag].innerHTML += message;
  else window[outputTag].innerHTML = message;
}


///// FILE: "Practice Level 3/controllers/gridSystemExample.js"

import { Column } from "../utils/Column.js";
import { GridSystem } from "../utils/GridSystem.js";
import { output } from "../utils/output.js";
import { Row } from "../utils/Row.js";

window.gridSystemExample = gridSystemExample;

export function gridSystemExample() {
  debugger;

  const gridSystem = new GridSystem();
  for (let rowNumber = 1; rowNumber <= 3; rowNumber++) {
    const row = new Row();

    for (let columnNumber = 1; columnNumber <= 3; columnNumber++) {
      const column = new Column(`COLUMN ${columnNumber}`);
      row.addColumn(column);
    }

    gridSystem.addRow(row);
  }

  output(gridSystem);
}

export class Column {
  openingTag = "<div class='col'>";
  closingTag = "</div>";

  }
}


///// FILE: "Practice Level 3/utils/GridSystem.js"

import { Row } from "./Row.js";

export class GridSystem {
  openingTag = "<div class='container'>";
  closingTag = "</div>";
  innerHTML = "";

  addRow(row = new Row()) {
    this.innerHTML += row;
  }
  toString() {
    return `${this.openingTag}${this.innerHTML}${this.closingTag}`;
  }
}


///// FILE: "Practice Level 3/utils/output.js"

export function output(
  message = "",
  outputTag = "outputTag",
  shouldAppend = true
) {
  if (shouldAppend) window[outputTag].innerHTML += message;
  else window[outputTag].innerHTML = message;
}


///// FILE: "Practice Level 3/utils/Row.js"

import { Column } from "./Column.js";

export class Row {
  openingTag = "<div class='row'>";
  closingTag = "</div>";
  innerHTML = "";

  addColumn(column = new Column()) {
    this.innerHTML += column;
  }

  toString() {
    return `${this.openingTag}${this.innerHTML}${this.closingTag}`;
  }
}
